shared_focus = {
	id = BOR_der_burgerkrieg
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_der_burgerkrieg_bormann
	cost = 0
	available = {
		always = no
	}
	allow_branch = {
		has_global_flag = german_civil_war
	}
	x = 8
	y = 0
	bypass = {
		has_global_flag = german_civil_war
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_der_burgerkrieg"
		custom_effect_tooltip = BOR_der_burgerkrieg_tt
	}
}

#Der Wilde Ritt - Bormann's wild ride begins!
shared_focus = {
	id = BOR_der_wilde_ritt
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_der_wilde_ritt
	allow_branch = { has_country_flag = BOR_Phase1 }
	cost = 3
	x = 0
	y = 0

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_der_wilde_ritt"
		country_event = bormann.0
		add_stability = 0.03
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_foreign_decisions_unlock_tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormannflavor.4 days = 9 } } # Schörner is pardoned
	}
	ai_will_do = { factor = 1000 }
}

#First Things First - Not really, he has to figure out boring stuff like food first.
shared_focus = {
	id = BOR_first_things_first
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_first_things_first
	cost = 3
	prerequisite = { focus = BOR_der_wilde_ritt }
	relative_position_id = BOR_der_wilde_ritt
	x = 0
	y = 1
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_first_things_first"
		add_political_power = 50
		TNO_improve_poverty_low = yes
		TNO_improve_pensions_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
		TNO_improve_unemployment_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.06 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		set_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = 0.75 }
		econ_inflation_change = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = bormannflavor.2 days = 3 } # Bormann has a talk with von Schirach
			country_event = { id = bormannflavor.3 days = 8 } # Bormann has a talk with Klopfer
		}
	}
}

#Notstandsrecht - Bormann reiterates the Führer's Notstandsrecht - his right to pass laws and make decisions without others input. He uses it wisely. For the best of Germany. Of course. No, really.
shared_focus = {
	id = BOR_notstandsrecht
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_notstandsrecht
	cost = 3
	prerequisite = { focus = BOR_slaves_to_farmers }
	prerequisite = { focus = BOR_soldiers_to_builders }
	relative_position_id = BOR_slaves_to_farmers
	x = 1
	y = 1
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_notstandsrecht"
		add_political_power = 100
		add_command_power = 5
		TNO_improve_political_parties_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
		admin_funding_maximal_increase_low = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip =  GER_BOR_reich_in_a_thousand_pieces_tooltip
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_BOR_the_reich_in_thousand_pieces_1_idea
			add_idea = GER_BOR_the_reich_in_thousand_pieces_2_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormannflavor.1 days = 5 } } # Bormann lifts smoking restrictions
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormannflavor.35 days = 10 } } # Iconoclasm Phase 1
	}
}

#U R B A N  S E C T I O N #

#Urban Reconstruction - Reconstruction of the settlements of Germany begins
shared_focus = {
	id = BOR_urban_reconstruction
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_urban_reconstruction
	cost = 3
	prerequisite = { focus = BOR_notstandsrecht }
	relative_position_id = BOR_notstandsrecht
	x = 0
	y = 1
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_urban_reconstruction"
		TNO_improve_poverty_med = yes
		add_stability = 0.1

		OR = {
			has_country_flag = BOR_militarists_dismantled
			has_country_flag = BOR_reformists_dismantled
		}
		CRI = { exists = no }
		UKR = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
		MCW = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
		CAU = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
	}
	ai_will_do = { #Only complete this focus after all other foci have been completed
		base = 0.05
	}
	prerequisite = { focus = BOR_waffenstillstand }
	relative_position_id = BOR_waffenstillstand
	x = 0
	y = 1
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_a_thousand_year_reich_forevermore"
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.25 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		effect_tooltip = { remove_ideas = GER_BOR_lost_generation_1_idea }
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = {
				GER_BOR_lost_generation_1_idea
				GER_BOR_lost_generation_2_idea
				GER_BOR_lost_generation_3_idea
				GER_BOR_lost_generation_4_idea
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = GER
				}
				add_ideas = GCW_hidden_credit_buff
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_socialism
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		TNO_improve_income_taxation_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
		TNO_improve_trade_laws_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
		clr_country_flag = BOR_Phase1
		set_country_flag = BOR_Phase2
		reload_GER_bormann_post_cw_tree = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BOR_schorner_okw }
				country_event = { id = bormannflavor.8 days = 20 } # Adenauer funeral
			}
			country_event = { id = bormannflavor.7 days = 80 } # The Bormann legacy
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormannflavor.18 days = 450 } } # Speer assassination chain
		}
	}
}

#    Bormann Example Tree(s)    #
#################################
#	Additional Information
#		Info relevant to above/listed
#	blahblahblah.

## <Status>; <Leader/Tagline> #		Distinct Section of Tree(s). I.e. separated "sub"tree or path etc.

##  # <Status>; <Tagline> #  ##		Distinct subsection of above tree. Implicit child of ^

### <Title>							Major nondistinct subsection. Implicit child of ^ and of Distinct Section

## <Title>							Minor nondistinct subsection. Implicit child of ^

#<Title/Info>						Note/Additional Info/Comment

#Examples below:

### Loyal; Calph von Calph ####
#von Calph can appear as a result of a rare event blah blah blah
#Bormann may fucking kill von Calph because he sucks

##  # Loyal; Bormann nice #  ##
#Bormann has chosen not to kill von Calph

### Introductory Section

## Right-hand Route; "Telegram for von Calph"
#<Insert Focuses>#

## Left-hand Route; "Honors for von Calph"
#<Insert Focuses>#

##   # SS; Bormann mean #   ##
#Bormann tried to kill von Calph


# Though it can appear excessive; this is the result of me trying to demonstrate the expected style 
# for Bormann code & commenting as quickly as possible, actual commenting will not be so excessive.
#
# You should be writing your code as if you are going to get hit over the head with a sledgehammer before morning
# and forget everything you did yesterday. If you choose to not do this;
# I will hit you with you a sledgehammer before morning and you will forget everything you did.
# Thanks.

###### Kaukasien; Revolt ######

shared_focus = { # Kaukasia blew up
	id = BOR_chaos_in_kaukasia
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_operation_schwarzes_gold
	cost = 1
	allow_branch = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = BOR_Phase1
				has_country_flag = GER_BOR_KAU_revolt
				NOT = { has_country_flag = BOR_DEBUG }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = BOR_DEBUG
				has_country_flag = BOR_DBG_KAU_revolt
			}
		}
	}
	x = 0
	y = 0
	relative_position_id = BOR_Kaukasien_Dummy

	will_lead_to_war_with = CAU
	will_lead_to_war_with = AZR
	will_lead_to_war_with = GEO
	will_lead_to_war_with = DAG
	will_lead_to_war_with = ADY

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_chaos_in_kaukasia"
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAU = {
					exists = yes
					has_country_flag = CAU_policy_business_plot
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAU_caucasian_anarchy }
				}
			}
			CAU = { save_party_popularities = yes }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = CAU
				autonomy_state = autonomy_autonomous_reichskommissariat
			}
			CAU = { apply_party_popularities = yes }

			if = { limit = { country_exists = AZR } declare_war_on = { target = AZR type = annex_everything } }
			if = { limit = { country_exists = GEO } declare_war_on = { target = GEO type = annex_everything } }
			if = { limit = { country_exists = DAG } declare_war_on = { target = DAG type = annex_everything } }
			if = { limit = { country_exists = ADY } declare_war_on = { target = ADY type = annex_everything } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { CAU = { exists = yes } }
			declare_war_on = { target = CAU type = annex_everything }
		}
		else = {
			if = { limit = { country_exists = AZR } declare_war_on = { target = AZR type = annex_everything } }
			if = { limit = { country_exists = GEO } declare_war_on = { target = GEO type = annex_everything } }
			if = { limit = { country_exists = DAG } declare_war_on = { target = DAG type = annex_everything } }
			if = { limit = { country_exists = ADY } declare_war_on = { target = ADY type = annex_everything } }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

			factor = 0
			has_country_flag = BOR_schorner_okw
		}
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_percentage = 0.015 }
		econ_GDP_boost_once_percentage = yes
	}
}

shared_focus = { # Now for Bormann's OUTLANDISH projects
	id = BOR_towards_greater_projects
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_wunderwaffe
	cost = 6
	prerequisite = {
		focus = BOR_a_national_renaissance
	}
	allow_branch = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = BOR_Closing
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = BOR_Herbst
					has_country_flag = BOR_DEBUG
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = BOR_DEBUG
				has_country_flag = BOR_DBG_Opulence
				NOT = { has_country_flag = BOR_DBG_Opulence_Herbst }
			}
		}
	}
	cancel = { 
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = herbst_begun
			has_country_flag = BOR_Herbst 
		} 
	}
	x = 0
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BOR_a_national_renaissance
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_towards_greater_projects"
		add_political_power = 100
	}
}

#A Thousand Year Wirtschaft - Germany's economic path for the forseeable future has been set!
shared_focus = {
	id = BOR_a_thousand_year_wirtschaft
	icon = GFX_focus_GER_thousand_year_wirtschaft
	cost = 5.00
	prerequisite = { 
		focus = BOR_mass_investment
		focus = BOR_mass_reinforcement
	}
	
	relative_position_id = BOR_mass_investment
	x = 1
	y = 1
	
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BOR_a_thousand_year_wirtschaft"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = BOR_mass_investment
			}
			
			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.035 }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
			
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.012 }
				econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
			}	
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_economic_reform_tooltip
	}
}
